Back Features HP ProBook 450 business laptop | HP® Official Store HP ProBook 450 Designed to power your workday Built for productivity, the HP ProBook 450 delivers the performance and security features essential for today's workforce. The sleek and tough design provides professionals a flexible platform to stay productive in or out of the office. Shop now Designed for mobility Work in style with the powerful 15.6-inch diagonal HP ProBook 450 with a new gravity black LCD cover. Confidently take on the day with an optional backlit,1 spill-resistant HP Premium Keyboard. Stay up and running HP Client Security HP Client Security2 suite helps you quickly and easily encrypt your hard drive, permanently delete unwanted or discarded data, restrict unauthorized access, and more. Trusted Platform Module The firmware Trusted Platform Module (TPM)3 provides hardware-based encryption keys to help secure your data, e-mail, and user credentials. HP Touchpoint Manager Avoid surprises by tracking device health and security policy enforcement. With the HP Touchpoint Manager app, IT can quickly address risks to keep devices functional, and employees productive.4 Built for performance Immersive experience Create a stunning visual and audio experience with options like an FHD display,1 an HD touch display,6 and DTS Studio Sound™. Reliable connections Stay connected with less interference using the built-in wireless support and optional Bluetooth® wireless technology.7 Windows 10 Pro Experience the new features of Windows 10 Pro5 on the thin, light, touch6 optional HP ProBook 450. Efficient storage options The latest storage options ensure optimum performance from your HP ProBook. Choose from a range of SSD, SSHD, and HDD drive options for up to 1TB of storage.8 Powerful processing Perform at your best with the latest 6th generation Intel® Core™ processors.9 Reliability you can trust Tested to go the distance During the HP Total Test Process, HP Pro PCs experience 120,000 hours of performance trials to help get you through your business day. Business PCs quality commitment Quality matters. Beginning with the design, HP builds quality into our products to deliver a positive customer experience from your initial purchase through the lifecycle of the product. Hardware TPM is v1.2, which is a subset of the TPM 2.0 specification version v0.89 as implemented by Intel Platform Trust Technology (PTT). HP Touchpoint Manager supports Android™, iOS and Windows operating systems and PCs, notebooks, tablets and smartphones from various manufacturers. Not available in all countries seeÂ www.hp.com/touchpointÂ for availability information. Touchpoint Manager requires purchase of a subscription. Out-of-band HP only Wipe, Lock, Unlock and reporting of BIOS boot error codes is available on select HP EliteBooks and select HP Elite x2 devices requires an internet connection, Intel® vPro™ technology and functions in S3/Sleep, S4/Hibernate and S5/Soft Off power states. SATA drives are wiped. The remote wipe of Self Encrypting Drives that have hardware encryption active is not supported. Some features require a Pro subscription. Not all features are available in all editions or versions of Windows. Systems may require upgraded and/or separately purchased hardware, drivers, software or BIOS update to take full advantage of Windows functionality. Windows 10 is automatically updated, which is always enabled. ISP fees may apply and additional requirements may apply over time for updates. Seehttp://www.microsoft.com. HD touchscreen is available as an optional feature. Wireless and Bluetooth may be optional features. Wireless requires separately purchased access point and internet service. Availability of public wireless access points limited. For storage drives, GB = 1 billion bytes. TB = 1 trillion bytes. Actual formatted capacity is less. Up to 16GB (for Windows 7) and up to 30GB (For Windows 8 and 10) are reserved for system recovery software. Up to 60GB is reserved for Windows 10 systems with >128GB of storage. Multi-Core is designed to improve performance of certain software products. Not all customers or software applications will necessarily benefit from use of this technology. 64-bit computing system required. Performance and clock frequency will vary depending on application workload and your hardware and software configurations. Intel's numbering is not a measurement of higher performance. The following applies to HP systems with Intel Skylake or next-generation silicon chip-based system shipping with Windows 7, Windows 8, Windows 8.1 or Windows 10 Pro systems downgraded to Windows 7 Professional, Windows 8 Pro, or Windows 8.1: This version of Windows running with the processor or chipsets used in this system has limited support from Microsoft.
